

===== FILE: templates\admin\form.html.twig =====

{% extends "base.html.twig" %}

{% block title %}{{ title }} - PinkShield{% endblock %}

{% block body %}
<div class="row justify-content-center">
    <div class="col-md-6">
        <div class="card shadow-lg">
            <div class="card-body p-5">
                <h2 class="mb-4">{{ title }}</h2>

                {{ form_start(form) }}
                    {% if form.vars.errors|length > 0 %}
                        <div class="alert alert-danger" role="alert">
                            <strong>Please fix the following errors:</strong>
                            <ul class="mb-0">
                                {% for error in form.vars.errors %}
                                    <li>{{ error.message }}</li>
                                {% endfor %}
                            </ul>
                        </div>
                    {% endif %}

                    <div class="mb-3">
                        {{ form_label(form.email) }}
                        {{ form_widget(form.email) }}
                        {% if form.email.vars.errors|length > 0 %}
                            <div class="invalid-feedback d-block">
                                {% for error in form.email.vars.errors %}
                                    {{ error.message }}
                                {% endfor %}
                            </div>
                        {% endif %}
                    </div>

                    <div class="mb-3">
                        {{ form_label(form.password) }}
                        {{ form_widget(form.password) }}
                        {% if form.password.vars.errors|length > 0 %}
                            <div class="invalid-feedback d-block">
                                {% for error in form.password.vars.errors %}
                                    {{ error.message }}
                                {% endfor %}
                            </div>
                        {% endif %}
                    </div>

                    <div class="d-grid gap-2">
                        <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">Save</button>
                        <a href="{% if form.vars.data.id %}{{ path('admin_index') }}{% else %}{{ path('login') }}{% endif %}" class="btn btn-secondary">Cancel</a>
                    </div>
                {{ form_end(form) }}
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
{% endblock %}

                        <a href="{{ path('admin_edit', {id: admin.id}) }}" class="btn btn-sm btn-warning">Edit</a>
                        <a href="{{ path('admin_delete', {id: admin.id}) }}" class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="return confirm('Are you sure?')">Delete</a>
                    </td>
                </tr>
            {% else %}
                <tr>
                    <td colspan="3" class="text-center">No admins found</td>

===== FILE: templates\admin\manage_blog.html.twig =====

{% extends "base.html.twig" %}

{% block title %}Manage Blog Posts - PinkShield{% endblock %}

{% block body %}
<div class="container mt-5">
    <div class="row mb-4">
        <div class="col-12">
            <h1 class="mb-4">
                <i class="fas fa-book"></i> Manage Blog Posts
            </h1>
        </div>
    </div>

    {% if app.flashes('success') %}
        {% for message in app.flashes('success') %}
            <div class="alert alert-success alert-dismissible fade show" role="alert">
                <i class="fas fa-check-circle me-2"></i>{{ message }}
                <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="alert"></button>
            </div>
        {% endfor %}
    {% endif %}

    <!-- Search and Sort Section -->
    <div class="card mb-4 shadow-sm">
        <div class="card-body">
            <div class="row g-3">
                <div class="col-md-6">
                    <form method="GET" class="d-flex gap-2" id="searchForm">
                        <input 
                            type="text" 
                            name="search" 
                            class="form-control" 
                            placeholder="Search by title, content, or author..." 
                            value="{{ search }}"
                        >
                        <input type="hidden" name="sortBy" value="{{ sortBy }}">
                        <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">
                            <i class="fas fa-search"></i> Search
                        </button>
                        {% if search %}
                            <a href="{{ path('admin_manage_blog', {'sortBy': sortBy}) }}" class="btn btn-secondary">
                                <i class="fas fa-times"></i> Clear
                            </a>
                        {% endif %}
                    </form>
                </div>
                <div class="col-md-6">
                    <form method="GET" class="d-flex gap-2">
                        <select name="sortBy" class="form-select" onchange="this.form.submit()">
                            <option value="date_newest" {% if sortBy == 'date_newest' %}selected{% endif %}>
                                <i class="fas fa-clock"></i> Newest First
                            </option>
                            <option value="date_oldest" {% if sortBy == 'date_oldest' %}selected{% endif %}>
                                <i class="fas fa-clock"></i> Oldest First
                            </option>
                            <option value="title_asc" {% if sortBy == 'title_asc' %}selected{% endif %}>
                                <i class="fas fa-sort-alpha-down"></i> Title A-Z
                            </option>
                            <option value="title_desc" {% if sortBy == 'title_desc' %}selected{% endif %}>
                                <i class="fas fa-sort-alpha-up"></i> Title Z-A
                            </option>
                            <option value="author" {% if sortBy == 'author' %}selected{% endif %}>
                                <i class="fas fa-user"></i> Author
                            </option>
                        </select>
                        <input type="hidden" name="search" value="{{ search }}">
                    </form>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Results Count -->
    <div class="mb-3">
        <span class="badge bg-info">{{ posts|length }} Post(s) Found</span>
        {% if search %}
            <span class="text-muted">Searching for: "<strong>{{ search }}</strong>"</span>
        {% endif %}
    </div>

    <!-- Blog Posts Table -->
    <div class="table-responsive">
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
            <thead class="table-dark">
                <tr>
                    <th>ID</th>
                    <th>Title</th>
                    <th>Author</th>
                    <th>Role</th>
                    <th>Created Date</th>
                    <th>Comments</th>
                    <th>Actions</th>
                </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
                {% if posts|length > 0 %}
                    {% for post in posts %}
                        <tr>
                            <td>#{{ post.id }}</td>
                            <td>
                                <strong>{{ post.title }}</strong>
                                {% if post.imagePath %}
                                    <i class="fas fa-image text-danger ms-2" title="Has image"></i>
                                {% endif %}
                            </td>
                            <td>{{ post.authorName }}</td>
                            <td>
                                <span class="badge bg-secondary">{{ post.authorRole }}</span>
                            </td>
                            <td>
                                <small>{{ post.createdAt|date('d/m/Y H:i') }}</small>
                            </td>
                            <td>
                                <span class="badge bg-info">{{ post.comments|length }}</span>
                            </td>
                            <td>
                                <a 
                                    href="{{ path('blog_show', {'id': post.id}) }}" 
                                    class="btn btn-sm btn-info"
                                    title="View Post"
                                >
                                    <i class="fas fa-eye"></i>
                                </a>
                                <form 
                                    method="POST" 
                                    style="display: inline;"
                                    onsubmit="return confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this post and all its comments?');"
                                >
                                    <input type="hidden" name="deleteId" value="{{ post.id }}">
                                    <button type="submit" class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" title="Delete Post">
                                        <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
                                    </button>
                                </form>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                    {% endfor %}
                {% else %}
                    <tr>
                        <td colspan="7" class="text-center py-4">
                            <i class="fas fa-inbox text-muted" style="font-size: 2rem;"></i>
                            <p class="text-muted mt-2">
                                {% if search %}
                                    No posts found matching "{{ search }}"
                                {% else %}
                                    No blog posts yet
                                {% endif %}
                            </p>
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                {% endif %}
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>

    <!-- Back Button -->
    <div class="mt-4">
        <a href="{{ path('admin_dashboard') }}" class="btn btn-secondary">
            <i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i> Back to Dashboard
        </a>
        <a href="{{ path('blog_new') }}" class="btn btn-primary">
            <i class="fas fa-plus"></i> Create New Post
        </a>
    </div>
</div>

<style>
    .table-responsive {
        border-radius: 0.5rem;
        box-shadow: 0 0.125rem 0.25rem rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.075);
    }

    .table {
        margin-bottom: 0;
    }

    .card {
        border: none;
    }

    .badge {
        padding: 0.5rem 0.75rem;
    }

    .btn-sm {
        padding: 0.375rem 0.75rem;
        font-size: 0.875rem;
    }
</style>
{% endblock %}

            <div class="card shadow-sm">
                <div class="card-header bg-primary text-white">

                </div>
                <div class="card-body">
                    <form method="post">
                        <div class="mb-3">
                            <label for="date" class="form-label">Date & Time</label>
                            <input type="datetime-local" name="date" id="date" class="form-control" value="{{ appointment.appointmentDate|date('Y-m-d\\TH:i') }}">
                        </div>
                        <div class="mb-3">
                            <label for="notes" class="form-label">Notes</label>
                            <textarea name="notes" id="notes" class="form-control" rows="4">{{ appointment.notes }}</textarea>
                        </div>
                        <div class="mb-3">
                            <label for="status" class="form-label">Status</label>
                            <select name="status" id="status" class="form-select">
                                <option value="pending" {% if appointment.status == 'pending' %}selected{% endif %}>Pending</option>
                                <option value="confirmed" {% if appointment.status == 'confirmed' %}selected{% endif %}>Confirmed</option>
                                <option value="cancelled" {% if appointment.status == 'cancelled' %}selected{% endif %}>Cancelled</option>
                            </select>
                        </div>
                        <div class="d-grid gap-2">
                            <button class="btn btn-primary">Save Changes</button>
                            <a href="{{ path('appointment_show', {'id': appointment.id}) }}" class="btn btn-secondary">Cancel</a>
                        </div>
                    </form>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
{% endblock %}

<div>
    {# Hero #}
    <div class="appt-hero">
        <div>
            <h1><i class="fas fa-calendar-check me-2" style="opacity:0.8;"></i>
                {% if is_granted('ROLE_ADMIN') %}All Appointments
                {% elseif is_granted('ROLE_DOCTOR') %}My Patient Appointments
                {% else %}My Appointments{% endif %}
            </h1>
            <p>Manage and track your medical consultations</p>
        </div>
        {% if is_granted('ROLE_USER') and not is_granted('ROLE_DOCTOR') and not is_granted('ROLE_ADMIN') %}
            <a href="{{ path('appointment_new') }}" class="btn btn-primary d-flex align-items-center gap-2">
                <i class="fas fa-calendar-plus"></i> Book Appointment
            </a>
        {% endif %}
    </div>

    <div class="view-tabs">

        </button>
        <button class="view-tab" data-target="calendar-view">
            <i class="fas fa-calendar-alt me-1"></i> Calendar View
        </button>
        {% if is_granted('ROLE_USER') and not is_granted('ROLE_DOCTOR') and not is_granted('ROLE_ADMIN') %}
        <button class="view-tab" data-target="ai-view">
            <i class="fas fa-brain me-1"></i> AI Suggestions
        </button>
        {% endif %}
    </div>

    {# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ LIST VIEW в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ #}
    <div id="list-view" class="view-section active">
        <div class="appt-panel">
            <div class="appt-panel-header">
                <h6><i class="fas fa-list me-2" style="color:var(--primary);"></i>Appointment List</h6>
                <span style="font-size:0.8rem;color:var(--text-muted);">{{ appointments|length }} record(s)</span>
            </div>

            {% if appointments|length > 0 %}
                <div class="table-responsive">
                    <table class="appt-table">
                        <thead>
                            <tr>
                                <th>Date & Time</th>
                                {% if is_granted('ROLE_DOCTOR') or is_granted('ROLE_ADMIN') %}<th>Patient</th>{% endif %}
                                {% if not is_granted('ROLE_DOCTOR') or is_granted('ROLE_ADMIN') %}<th>Doctor</th>{% endif %}
                                <th>Status</th>
                                <th>Notes</th>
                                <th>Actions</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody>
                            {% for appointment in appointments %}
                                <tr>

{% block javascripts %}
<script src='https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/fullcalendar@6.1.9/index.global.min.js'></script>
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // в”Җв”Җв”Җ Tab Switching в”Җв”Җв”Җ
    document.querySelectorAll('.view-tab').forEach(function(tab) {
        tab.addEventListener('click', function() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.view-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
            document.querySelectorAll('.view-section').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
            this.classList.add('active');
            document.getElementById(this.dataset.target).classList.add('active');

            // Initialize calendar when shown (FullCalendar needs visible container)
            if (this.dataset.target === 'calendar-view' && !window._calendarInitialized) {
                initCalendar();
                window._calendarInitialized = true;
            }
        });
    });

    // в”Җв”Җв”Җ FullCalendar в”Җв”Җв”Җ
    function initCalendar() {
        var calendarEl = document.getElementById('fullCalendar');
        var calendar = new FullCalendar.Calendar(calendarEl, {
            initialView: 'dayGridMonth',
            headerToolbar: {
                left: 'prev,next today',
                center: 'title',
                right: 'dayGridMonth,timeGridWeek,timeGridDay,listWeek'
            },
            height: 'auto',
            navLinks: true,
            editable: false,
            selectable: false,
            eventClick: function(info) {
                window.location.href = '/appointment/' + info.event.id;
            },
            events: function(fetchInfo, successCallback, failureCallback) {
                fetch('{{ path("fc_load_events") }}')
                    .then(function(response) { return response.json(); })
                    .then(function(data) { successCallback(data); })
                    .catch(function(error) {
                        console.error('Error loading events:', error);
                        failureCallback(error);
                    });
            }
        });
        calendar.render();
    }
});

// в”Җв”Җв”Җ Buy Product (Stripe checkout) в”Җв”Җв”Җ
function buyProduct(productName) {
    if (!confirm('Purchase ' + productName + '?')) return;

    fetch('{{ path("appointment_checkout_product") }}', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ productName: productName })
    })
    .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
    .then(function(data) {
        if (data.checkoutUrl) {
            window.location.href = data.checkoutUrl;
        } else {
            alert(data.error || 'Could not start checkout.');
        }
    })
    .catch(function(e) {
        alert('Error: ' + e.message);
    });
}
</script>
{% endblock %}

.face-feedback.captured { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; background: rgba(16,185,129,0.1); color: #10b981; border: 1px solid rgba(16,185,129,0.2); }
.face-feedback.scanning { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; background: rgba(37,99,235,0.1); color: #60a5fa; border: 1px solid rgba(37,99,235,0.2); }
.face-feedback.error    { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; background: rgba(220,53,69,0.1); color: #ff6b6b; border: 1px solid rgba(220,53,69,0.2); }
.face-feedback.success  { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; background: rgba(16,185,129,0.1); color: #10b981; border: 1px solid rgba(16,185,129,0.2); }

{% block javascripts %}
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

    // в”Җв”Җ Starfield particles в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    const sf = document.getElementById('starfield');
    for (let i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
        const p = document.createElement('div');
        p.className = 'particle';
        const size = Math.random() * 3 + 1;
        p.style.cssText = `
            width:${size}px; height:${size}px;
            left:${Math.random()*100}%;
            background:${Math.random()>0.7 ? '#c0396b' : Math.random()>0.5 ? '#60a5fa' : '#fff'};
            animation-duration:${Math.random()*15+8}s;
            animation-delay:${Math.random()*10}s;
            box-shadow:0 0 ${size*3}px currentColor;
        `;
        sf.appendChild(p);
    }

    // в”Җв”Җ Password toggle в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    const togglePw   = document.getElementById('togglePw');
    const pwInput    = document.getElementById('inputPassword');
    const toggleIcon = document.getElementById('togglePwIcon');
    if (togglePw) {
        togglePw.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const isPass = pwInput.type === 'password';
            pwInput.type = isPass ? 'text' : 'password';
            toggleIcon.className = isPass ? 'fas fa-eye-slash' : 'fas fa-eye';
        });
    }

    // в”Җв”Җ Standard AJAX validation в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    const form = document.getElementById('loginForm');
    if (form && typeof AjaxValidator !== 'undefined') {
        AjaxValidator.attachBlur(form);
        AjaxValidator.attachSubmit(form, null, function () {
            form.removeEventListener('submit', null);
            form.submit();
        });
    }

    // в”Җв”Җ 3D tilt on glass card в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    const card = document.querySelector('.glass-card');
    if (card) {
        card.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
            const r  = card.getBoundingClientRect();
            const x  = (e.clientX - r.left) / r.width  - 0.5;
            const y  = (e.clientY - r.top)  / r.height - 0.5;
            card.style.transform = `perspective(800px) rotateY(${x*6}deg) rotateX(${-y*6}deg) translateY(-4px)`;
        });
        card.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
            card.style.transform = '';
        });
    }

    // в”Җв”Җ Face Recognition в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    const video        = document.getElementById('loginWebcamVideo');
    const canvas       = document.getElementById('loginCapturedCanvas');
    const btnOpen      = document.getElementById('loginBtnOpen');
    const btnCapture   = document.getElementById('loginBtnCapture');
    const btnRetake    = document.getElementById('loginBtnRetake');
    const fileInput    = document.getElementById('loginFaceFileInput');
    const btnFaceLogin = document.getElementById('btnFaceLogin');
    const feedback     = document.getElementById('loginFaceFeedback');
    const feedbackMsg  = document.getElementById('loginFaceMsg');
    const emailInput   = document.getElementById('inputUsername');

    let stream = null, capturedBlob = null;

    function setFeedback(type, msg, icon='') {
        feedback.className = 'face-feedback ' + type;
        feedbackMsg.textContent = msg;
        if (icon) feedback.querySelector('i').className = icon;
    }
    function stopStream() {
        if (stream) { stream.getTracks().forEach(t => t.stop()); stream = null; }
    }
    function showCanvas() {
        video.style.display='none'; canvas.style.display='block';
        btnCapture.style.display='none'; btnRetake.style.display='inline-flex'; btnOpen.style.display='none';
        stopStream();
    }
    function showVideo() {
        video.style.display='block'; canvas.style.display='none';
        btnCapture.style.display='inline-flex'; btnRetake.style.display='none';
    }

    btnOpen.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        try {
            stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ video: { facingMode: 'user' } });
            video.srcObject = stream;
            video.style.display = 'block';
            btnCapture.disabled = false;
            btnOpen.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-video"></i> On';
            btnOpen.style.opacity = '0.5';
        } catch (err) {
            alert('Camera denied: ' + err.message + '\n\nUse Upload Photo instead.');
        }
    });

    btnCapture.addEventListener('click', () => {
        canvas.width = video.videoWidth || 320;
        canvas.height = video.videoHeight || 240;
        canvas.getContext('2d').drawImage(video, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
        showCanvas();
        canvas.toBlob(b => {
            capturedBlob = b;
            btnFaceLogin.disabled = false;
            setFeedback('captured', 'Photo captured вҖ” ready to sign in', 'fas fa-check-circle');
        }, 'image/jpeg', 0.92);
    });

    btnRetake.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        capturedBlob = null;
        btnFaceLogin.disabled = true;
        feedback.className = 'face-feedback';
        showVideo();
        btnCapture.disabled = true;
        btnOpen.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-video"></i> Open';
        btnOpen.style.opacity = '';
        btnOpen.click();
    });

    fileInput.addEventListener('change', () => {
        if (!fileInput.files.length) return;
        capturedBlob = fileInput.files[0];
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = e => {
            const img = new Image();
            img.onload = () => {
                canvas.width = img.width; canvas.height = img.height;
                canvas.getContext('2d').drawImage(img, 0, 0);
                showCanvas();
            };
            img.src = e.target.result;
        };
        reader.readAsDataURL(capturedBlob);
        btnFaceLogin.disabled = false;
        setFeedback('captured', 'Photo loaded вҖ” ready to sign in', 'fas fa-check-circle');
    });

    btnFaceLogin.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const email = emailInput ? emailInput.value.trim() : '';
        if (!email) {
            setFeedback('error', 'Enter your email address above first.', 'fas fa-exclamation-circle');
            emailInput && emailInput.focus(); return;
        }
        if (!capturedBlob) {
            setFeedback('error', 'Capture or upload a photo first.', 'fas fa-exclamation-circle'); return;
        }
        setFeedback('scanning', 'Scanning face, please waitвҖҰ', 'fas fa-spinner fa-spin');
        btnFaceLogin.disabled = true;

        const fd = new FormData();
        fd.append('email', email);
        fd.append('face_photo', capturedBlob instanceof File
            ? capturedBlob
            : new File([capturedBlob], 'face_login.jpg', { type: 'image/jpeg' }));

        try {
            const res  = await fetch('/face-login', { method: 'POST', body: fd });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) {
                setFeedback('success', 'Face verified! RedirectingвҖҰ', 'fas fa-check-circle');
                setTimeout(() => { window.location.href = data.redirect || '/'; }, 800);
            } else {
                setFeedback('error', data.message || 'Face not recognized.', 'fas fa-times-circle');
                btnFaceLogin.disabled = false;
            }
        } catch (err) {
            setFeedback('error', 'Network error. Please try again.', 'fas fa-times-circle');
            btnFaceLogin.disabled = false;
        }
    });

    // в”Җв”Җ Scroll reveal в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach(e => {
            if (e.isIntersecting) {
                e.target.style.opacity = '1';
                e.target.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
            }
        });
    }, { threshold: 0.1 });

    document.querySelectorAll('.field-group, .btn-signin, .or-divider, .face-section, .register-row').forEach(el => {
        el.style.opacity = '0';
        el.style.transform = 'translateY(20px)';
        el.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease, transform 0.5s ease';
        observer.observe(el);
    });
});
</script>
{% endblock %}

<script>
// Stars
(function() {
    const c = document.getElementById('regStars');
    if (!c) return;
    for (let i = 0; i < 80; i++) {
        const s = document.createElement('div');
        const sz = Math.random() * 2 + 0.5;
        s.className = 'reg-star';
        s.style.cssText = `width:${sz}px;height:${sz}px;top:${Math.random()*100}%;left:${Math.random()*100}%;--d:${2+Math.random()*3}s;--delay:${Math.random()*4}s;opacity:0.3`;
        c.appendChild(s);
    }
})();

// Toggle Patient/Doctor
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const patientRadio  = document.getElementById('patient_type');
    const doctorRadio   = document.getElementById('doctor_type');
    const patientBtn    = document.getElementById('patient_register_btn');
    const doctorBtn     = document.getElementById('doctor_register_btn');
    const patientDesc   = document.getElementById('patient_desc');
    const doctorDesc    = document.getElementById('doctor_desc');

    function updateUI() {
        const isDoctor = doctorRadio.checked;
        patientBtn.style.display  = isDoctor ? 'none' : 'block';
        doctorBtn.style.display   = isDoctor ? 'block' : 'none';
        patientDesc.style.display = isDoctor ? 'none' : 'block';
        doctorDesc.style.display  = isDoctor ? 'block' : 'none';
    }

    patientRadio.addEventListener('change', updateUI);
    doctorRadio.addEventListener('change', updateUI);
});
</script>
{% endblock %}

{% block javascripts %}
<script>
(function () {
    const pwBtn = document.getElementById('doctorPwToggle');
    const pwInput = document.getElementById('doctor_password');
    if (pwBtn && pwInput) {
        pwBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
            const icon = this.querySelector('i');
            if (pwInput.type === 'password') {
                pwInput.type = 'text';
                icon.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash';
            } else {
                pwInput.type = 'password';
                icon.className = 'fas fa-eye';
            }
        });
    }

    const form = document.getElementById('doctorRegForm');
    if (form) {
        AjaxValidator.attachBlur(form);
        AjaxValidator.attachSubmit(form);
    }
})();
</script>
{% endblock %}

{% block javascripts %}
<script>
(function () {
    // в”Җв”Җ Password toggle в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    const pwBtn   = document.getElementById('patientPwToggle');
    const pwInput = document.getElementById('patient_password');
    if (pwBtn && pwInput) {
        pwBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
            const icon = this.querySelector('i');
            if (pwInput.type === 'password') {
                pwInput.type = 'text';
                icon.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash';
            } else {
                pwInput.type = 'password';
                icon.className = 'fas fa-eye';
            }
        });
    }

    // в”Җв”Җ AjaxValidator в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    const form = document.getElementById('patientRegForm');
    if (form) {
        AjaxValidator.attachBlur(form);
        AjaxValidator.attachSubmit(form);
    }

    // в”Җв”Җ Face Recognition в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
    const video          = document.getElementById('webcamVideo');
    const canvas         = document.getElementById('capturedCanvas');
    const btnOpen        = document.getElementById('btnOpenCamera');
    const btnCapture     = document.getElementById('btnCapture');
    const btnRetake      = document.getElementById('btnRetake');
    const faceFileInput  = document.getElementById('faceFileInput');   // manual upload
    const hiddenInput    = document.getElementById('facePhotoHidden'); // sent to server
    const faceStatus     = document.getElementById('faceStatus');
    let   stream         = null;

    /** Convert a canvas/blob to a File and inject into the hidden input */
    function attachFileToHidden(blob, name) {
        const file = new File([blob], name, { type: 'image/jpeg' });
        const dt   = new DataTransfer();
        dt.items.add(file);
        hiddenInput.files = dt.files;
        faceStatus.className = 'face-status captured';
        faceStatus.style.display = '';
    }

    function stopStream() {
        if (stream) {
            stream.getTracks().forEach(t => t.stop());
            stream = null;
        }
    }

    function showCanvasCapture() {
        video.style.display   = 'none';
        canvas.style.display  = 'block';
        btnCapture.style.display = 'none';
        btnRetake.style.display  = 'inline-flex';
        btnOpen.style.display    = 'none';
        stopStream();
    }

    function showVideo() {
        video.style.display   = 'block';
        canvas.style.display  = 'none';
        btnCapture.style.display = 'inline-flex';
        btnRetake.style.display  = 'none';
    }

    /** Open webcam */
    btnOpen.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        try {
            stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ video: { facingMode: 'user' } });
            video.srcObject = stream;
            video.style.display = 'block';
            btnCapture.disabled = false;
            btnOpen.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-video"></i> Camera On';
            btnOpen.style.opacity = '0.6';
        } catch (err) {
            alert('Unable to access camera: ' + err.message + '\n\nPlease use the "Upload Photo" button instead.');
        }
    });

    /** Capture frame from webcam */
    btnCapture.addEventListener('click', () => {
        canvas.width  = video.videoWidth  || 320;
        canvas.height = video.videoHeight || 240;
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
        showCanvasCapture();
        canvas.toBlob(blob => attachFileToHidden(blob, 'webcam_capture.jpg'), 'image/jpeg', 0.92);
    });

    /** Retake вҖ” restart camera */
    btnRetake.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        hiddenInput.value = '';
        faceStatus.style.display = 'none';
        showVideo();
        btnCapture.disabled = true;
        btnOpen.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-video"></i> Open Camera';
        btnOpen.style.opacity = '';
        // re-open camera
        btnOpen.click();
    });

    /** Manual file upload fallback */
    faceFileInput.addEventListener('change', () => {
        if (!faceFileInput.files.length) return;
        const file = faceFileInput.files[0];
        // Show preview in canvas
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = e => {
            const img = new Image();
            img.onload = () => {
                canvas.width  = img.width;
                canvas.height = img.height;
                canvas.getContext('2d').drawImage(img, 0, 0);
                showCanvasCapture();
            };
            img.src = e.target.result;
        };
        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
        // Attach directly to hidden input
        const dt = new DataTransfer();
        dt.items.add(file);
        hiddenInput.files = dt.files;
        faceStatus.className = 'face-status captured';
        faceStatus.style.display = '';
    });
})();
</script>
{% endblock %}

<script>
function togglePw(id, btn) {
    const input = document.getElementById(id);
    const icon = btn.querySelector('i');
    if (input.type === 'password') {
        input.type = 'text';
        icon.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash';
    } else {
        input.type = 'password';
        icon.className = 'fas fa-eye';
    }
}

const pwInput   = document.getElementById('password');
const confInput = document.getElementById('confirm_password');
const bar       = document.getElementById('strengthBar');
const label     = document.getElementById('strengthLabel');
const matchMsg  = document.getElementById('matchMsg');
const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
const resetForm = document.getElementById('resetForm');

function getStrength(pw) {
    let score = 0;
    if (pw.length >= 8)  score++;
    if (pw.length >= 10) score++;
    if (/[A-Z]/.test(pw)) score++;
    if (/[0-9]/.test(pw)) score++;
    if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(pw)) score++;
    return score;
}

pwInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
    const pw = pwInput.value;
    const score = getStrength(pw);
    const widths = ['0%', '20%', '40%', '65%', '85%', '100%'];
    const colors = ['#e5e7eb', '#ef4444', '#f59e0b', '#3b82f6', '#4CAF87', '#16a34a'];
    const labels = ['', 'TrГЁs faible', 'Faible', 'Moyen', 'Fort', 'TrГЁs fort'];
    bar.style.width = widths[score];
    bar.style.background = colors[score];
    label.textContent = pw.length ? labels[score] : '';
    label.style.color = colors[score];
    updateSubmitState();
});

confInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
    updateSubmitState();
});

function updateSubmitState() {
    const pw = pwInput.value;
    const conf = confInput.value;
    
    // Check match
    if (pw && conf) {
        matchMsg.style.display = 'block';
        if (pw === conf) {
            matchMsg.textContent = 'вң“ Les mots de passe correspondent';
            matchMsg.style.color = '#16a34a';
        } else {
            matchMsg.textContent = 'вң— Les mots de passe ne correspondent pas';
            matchMsg.style.color = '#ef4444';
        }
    } else {
        matchMsg.style.display = 'none';
    }

    // Enable if both non-empty (AJAX will handle complex server-side validation on blur/submit)
    submitBtn.disabled = !(pw.length > 0 && conf.length > 0);
}

// Initial state
updateSubmitState();

/* AjaxValidator setup moved to javascripts block below */
</script>
{% endblock %}

{% block javascripts %}
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    AjaxValidator.attachBlur(resetForm, function (input) {
        if (input.dataset.ajaxValidate === 'confirm_password') {
            return pwInput.value;
        }
        return '';
    });
    AjaxValidator.attachSubmit(resetForm, function (input) {
        if (input.dataset.ajaxValidate === 'confirm_password') {
            return pwInput.value;
        }
        return '';
    });
});
</script>

        {# Collapse navbar on mobile link click #}
        <script>
            document.querySelectorAll('.navbar-collapse a:not(.dropdown-toggle)').forEach(link => {
                link.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    const collapse = document.querySelector('.navbar-collapse');
                    if (collapse?.classList.contains('show')) {
                        bootstrap.Collapse.getInstance(collapse)?.hide();
                    }
                });
            });
        </script>

        {# Sidebar toggle logic #}
        {% if app.user %}
        <script>
            (function () {
                const sidebar   = document.getElementById('sidebar');
                const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('sidebarToggle');
                const icon      = toggleBtn ? toggleBtn.querySelector('i') : null;
                const MOBILE_BP = 992;
                const KEY       = 'ps_sidebar_open';

                function isDesktop() { return window.innerWidth >= MOBILE_BP; }

                function applyState(open) {
                    if (open) {
                        sidebar.classList.add('show');
                        toggleBtn.style.left = 'calc(var(--sidebar-width) + 10px)';
                    } else {
                        sidebar.classList.remove('show');
                        toggleBtn.style.left = '12px';
                    }
                    if (icon) {
                        icon.className = open ? 'fas fa-times' : 'fas fa-bars';
                    }
                }

                // Initial state
                const stored = localStorage.getItem(KEY);
                let open = isDesktop() ? (stored !== 'false') : (stored === 'true');
                applyState(open);

                toggleBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    open = !open;
                    localStorage.setItem(KEY, open);
                    applyState(open);
                });

                window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
                    open = isDesktop() ? (localStorage.getItem(KEY) !== 'false') : false;
                    applyState(open);
                });

                // Close sidebar on mobile when a sidebar link is clicked
                if (!isDesktop()) {
                    sidebar.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-link').forEach(link => {
                        link.addEventListener('click', () => {
                            open = false;
                            applyState(false);
                        });
                    });
                }
            })();
        </script>
        {% endif %}

        {# Notification loader #}
        {% if app.user %}
        <script>
            /* -- Time Ago helper ------------------------------- */
            function notifTimeAgo(ts) {
                const secs = Math.floor((Date.now() / 1000) - ts);
                const intervals = [
                    { l: 'y',  s: 31536000 }, { l: 'mo', s: 2592000 },
                    { l: 'w',  s: 604800 },   { l: 'd',  s: 86400 },
                    { l: 'h',  s: 3600 },     { l: 'm',  s: 60 },
                ];
                for (const i of intervals) {
                    const c = Math.floor(secs / i.s);
                    if (c >= 1) return `${c}${i.l} ago`;
                }
                return 'now';
            }

            const typeColors = {
                info:    { bg: '#dbeafe', color: '#2563eb' },
                success: { bg: '#dcfce7', color: '#16a34a' },
                warning: { bg: '#fef3c7', color: '#d97706' },
                danger:  { bg: '#fee2e2', color: '#dc2626' },
            };

            function loadNotifications() {
                const badgeEl = document.getElementById('notificationBadge');
                if (!badgeEl) return;

                fetch('{{ path('notifications_api_list') }}')
                    .then(r => { if (!r.ok) throw new Error(); return r.json(); })
                    .then(data => {
                        if (!data?.notifications) return;

                        const unreadEl    = document.getElementById('unreadCount');
                        const containerEl = document.getElementById('notificationsContainer');
                        const count       = data.unreadCount ?? 0;

                        // Badge
                        if (count > 0) {
                            badgeEl.textContent = count > 9 ? '9+' : count;
                            badgeEl.style.display = 'block';
                        } else {
                            badgeEl.style.display = 'none';
                        }

                        if (unreadEl) {
                            unreadEl.textContent = count > 0 ? `${count} new` : '';
                        }

                        if (containerEl) {
                            if (data.notifications.length === 0) {
                                containerEl.innerHTML = `
                                    <li class="text-center py-4 text-muted">
                                        <i class="fas fa-check-circle d-block mb-2" style="font-size:1.5rem;color:#d1d5db;"></i>
                                        <small>All caught up!</small>
                                    </li>`;
                            } else {
                                const showUrlTpl = '{{ path('notification_show', {id: 0}) }}';
                                containerEl.innerHTML = data.notifications.slice(0, 5).map(n => {
                                    const url  = showUrlTpl.replace('0', n.id);
                                    const tc   = typeColors[n.type] || typeColors.info;
                                    const time = n.timestamp ? notifTimeAgo(n.timestamp) : n.createdAt;
                                    return `<li>
                                        <a href="${url}" class="dropdown-item px-3 py-2" style="white-space:normal;border-left:3px solid ${tc.color};${n.isRead?'':'background:rgba(76,175,135,0.04);'}">
                                            <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;align-items:flex-start;">
                                                <span style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:8px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:0.85rem;flex-shrink:0;background:${tc.bg};color:${tc.color};">
                                                    <i class="${n.icon}"></i>
                                                </span>
                                                <div style="min-width:0;">
                                                    <div style="font-size:0.82rem;font-weight:${n.isRead?'500':'700'};color:#1f2937;line-height:1.3;">${n.title}</div>
                                                    <div style="font-size:0.76rem;color:#6b7280;margin-top:2px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;display:-webkit-box;-webkit-line-clamp:2;-webkit-box-orient:vertical;">${n.message}</div>
                                                    <div style="font-size:0.7rem;color:#9ca3af;margin-top:3px;"><i class="far fa-clock me-1"></i>${time}</div>
                                                </div>
                                                ${!n.isRead ? '<span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--primary);flex-shrink:0;margin-top:4px;"></span>' : ''}
                                            </div>
                                        </a>
                                    </li>`;
                                }).join('');
                            }
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(() => {});
            }

            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', loadNotifications);
            setInterval(loadNotifications, 30000);
        </script>
        {% endif %}

        {# -- AI Chatbot Widget (shown only to logged-in users) ---------------- #}
        {% if app.user %}
        <style>
            /* -- Chatbot Container ------------------------------------------- */
            #ps-chatbot-wrapper {
                position: fixed;
                bottom: 28px;

                z-index: 9999;
                display: flex;

            /* -- Toggle Button ----------------------------------------------- */
            #ps-chat-toggle {

                border-radius: 50%;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #c0396b 0%, #e8557a 100%);
                border: none;
                color: #fff;
                font-size: 1.35rem;
                display: flex;
                align-items: center;
                justify-content: center;
                cursor: pointer;
                box-shadow: 0 6px 24px rgba(192, 57, 107, 0.45);
                transition: all 0.25s ease;
                position: relative;
                flex-shrink: 0;
            }

            #ps-chat-toggle:hover {
                transform: scale(1.1);
                box-shadow: 0 8px 32px rgba(192, 57, 107, 0.60);
            }

            #ps-chat-toggle .ps-toggle-icon { transition: transform 0.25s ease; }
            #ps-chat-toggle.open .ps-toggle-icon { transform: rotate(90deg); }

            /* Unread badge on toggle */
            #ps-chat-unread {
                position: absolute;
                top: -2px;
                right: -2px;
                width: 16px;
                height: 16px;
                background: #ef4444;
                border-radius: 50%;
                font-size: 0.6rem;
                font-weight: 700;
                color: #fff;
                display: none;
                align-items: center;
                justify-content: center;
                border: 2px solid #fff;

            /* -- Chat Panel -------------------------------------------------- */

            }

        <!-- Chatbot HTML -->
        <div id="ps-chatbot-wrapper">
            <!-- Chat Panel -->
            <div id="ps-chat-panel" role="dialog" aria-label="PinkShield AI Assistant">
                <!-- Header -->

                    <div class="ps-chat-avatar">??</div>
                    <div class="ps-chat-header-info">
                        <div class="ps-chat-header-name">PinkShield AI</div>
                        <div class="ps-chat-header-status">
                            <span class="ps-status-dot"></span> Online · AI Health Assistant
                        </div>

                    <button class="ps-chat-close" id="ps-close-btn" aria-label="Close chat">
                        <i class="fas fa-times"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>

                <!-- Messages -->
                <div class="ps-chat-messages" id="ps-chat-messages"></div>

                <!-- Quick Suggestions -->
                <div class="ps-suggestions" id="ps-suggestions">
                    <button class="ps-suggestion-btn" data-msg="Book an appointment">?? Book appointment</button>
                    <button class="ps-suggestion-btn" data-msg="Health tips">?? Health tips</button>
                    <button class="ps-suggestion-btn" data-msg="What is PinkShield?">?? About</button>
                    <button class="ps-suggestion-btn" data-msg="Help">? Help</button>
                </div>

                <!-- Input -->
                <div class="ps-chat-input-area">
                    <input
                        type="text"
                        id="ps-chat-input"
                        placeholder="Ask me anything about health..."
                        autocomplete="off"
                        maxlength="500"
                        aria-label="Chat message"
                    >
                    <button id="ps-chat-send" aria-label="Send message">
                        <i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Toggle Button -->
            <button id="ps-chat-toggle" aria-label="Toggle AI chat assistant">
                <span class="ps-toggle-icon"><i class="fas fa-comment-medical"></i></span>
                <span id="ps-chat-unread" style="display:none;"></span>

        {# Pass username safely via data attribute #}
        <div id="ps-chat-data" 
             data-username="{{ app.user.userIdentifier|split('@')|first }}"
             style="display:none;"></div>

        <script type="module">
        import * as webllm from "https://esm.run/@mlc-ai/web-llm";

        (function () {
            // -- DOM refs ----------------------------------------------------
            const panel     = document.getElementById('ps-chat-panel');
            const toggle    = document.getElementById('ps-chat-toggle');
            const closeBtn  = document.getElementById('ps-close-btn');
            const messages  = document.getElementById('ps-chat-messages');
            const input     = document.getElementById('ps-chat-input');
            const sendBtn   = document.getElementById('ps-chat-send');
            const sugDiv    = document.getElementById('ps-suggestions');
            const headerStatus = panel.querySelector('.ps-chat-header-status');

            // -- State -------------------------------------------------------
            let isOpen       = false;
            let hasWelcome   = false;
            let isBusy       = false;
            let engine       = null;
            let modelReady   = false;
            let modelLoading = false;
            const history    = [];   // conversation memory

            // -- WebLLM config -----------------------------------------------
            const MODEL_ID = "Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct-q4f16_1-MLC";
            const SYSTEM_PROMPT = `You are PinkShield AI, a warm and professional AI health assistant for the PinkShield medical management platform. You help patients with health questions, booking information, wellness tips, and navigating the platform. Keep answers concise (2-4 sentences max unless asked for more). Be empathetic and encouraging. For emergencies always say to call emergency services. Never diagnose — always recommend consulting a doctor for personal medical issues. Respond in the same language the user writes in.`;

            // -- Open / Close ------------------------------------------------
            function openChat() {
                isOpen = true;
                panel.classList.add('open');
                toggle.classList.add('open');
                toggle.querySelector('.ps-toggle-icon').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-times"></i>';
                if (!hasWelcome) { showWelcome(); hasWelcome = true; }
                if (!modelReady && !modelLoading) loadModel();
                setTimeout(() => input.focus(), 300);
            }

            function closeChat() {
                isOpen = false;
                panel.classList.remove('open');
                toggle.classList.remove('open');
                toggle.querySelector('.ps-toggle-icon').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-comment-medical"></i>';
            }

            toggle.addEventListener('click', () => isOpen ? closeChat() : openChat());
            closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeChat);

            // -- Welcome message ---------------------------------------------
            function showWelcome() {
                const dataEl   = document.getElementById('ps-chat-data');
                const userName = dataEl ? (dataEl.dataset.username || 'there') : 'there';
                addBotMsg(`?? Hello, **${userName}**! I'm **PinkShield AI**, powered by a real AI model running directly in your browser.\n\n?? The AI model is loading... This may take a minute the **first time** (it downloads and caches locally). After that it starts instantly!\n\nFeel free to ask me anything about your health or our platform.`);
            }

            // -- Load WebLLM model with progress -----------------------------
            async function loadModel() {
                modelLoading = true;
                input.disabled = true;
                sendBtn.disabled = true;
                input.placeholder = 'AI is loading...';

                // Show progress bar in header
                setHeaderStatus('? Downloading AI model...');

                try {
                    engine = await webllm.CreateMLCEngine(MODEL_ID, {
                        initProgressCallback: (progress) => {
                            const pct = Math.round((progress.progress || 0) * 100);
                            setHeaderStatus(`? Loading ${pct}%`);
                        },
                    });
                    modelReady   = true;
                    modelLoading = false;
                    input.disabled = false;
                    sendBtn.disabled = false;
                    input.placeholder = 'Ask me anything about health...';
                    setHeaderStatus('?? AI Ready · Ask me anything!');
                    addBotMsg('? **AI model loaded!** I\'m fully operational now. What would you like to know?');
                    setTimeout(() => setHeaderStatus('<span class="ps-status-dot"></span> Online · AI by WebLLM'), 4000);
                } catch (err) {
                    modelLoading = false;
                    input.disabled = false;
                    input.placeholder = 'Ask me anything about health...';
                    setHeaderStatus('?? WebGPU not supported');
                    addBotMsg('?? **Your browser does not support WebGPU**, which is required to run the local AI model.\n\nPlease use **Chrome 113+** or **Edge 113+** for full AI support.\n\nI\'ll still try to help with basic answers!');
                    console.error('WebLLM init error:', err);
                }
            }

            // -- Add messages -------------------------------------------------
            function addBotMsg(text) {
                const el = createBubble('bot', renderMarkdown(text));
                messages.appendChild(el);
                scrollBottom();
                return el;
            }

            function addUserMsg(text) {
                const el = createBubble('user', escapeHtml(text));
                messages.appendChild(el);
                scrollBottom();
            }

            function createBubble(role, html) {
                const wrap = document.createElement('div');
                wrap.className = `ps-msg ${role}`;
                wrap.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="ps-msg-avatar">${role === 'bot' ? '??' : '??'}</div>
                    <div class="ps-msg-bubble">${html}</div>
                `;
                return wrap;
            }

            // -- Typing indicator ---------------------------------------------
            function showTyping() {
                const el = document.createElement('div');
                el.className = 'ps-msg bot';
                el.id = 'ps-typing-indicator';
                el.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="ps-msg-avatar">??</div>
                    <div class="ps-msg-bubble">
                        <div class="ps-typing"><span></span><span></span><span></span></div>
                    </div>
                `;
                messages.appendChild(el);
                scrollBottom();
            }

            function hideTyping() {
                const el = document.getElementById('ps-typing-indicator');
                if (el) el.remove();
            }

            // -- Send message with streaming ----------------------------------
            async function sendMessage(text) {
                text = text.trim();
                if (!text || isBusy) return;

                isBusy = true;
                sendBtn.disabled = true;
                sugDiv.style.display = 'none';
                input.value = '';

                addUserMsg(text);
                history.push({ role: 'user', content: text });

                if (!modelReady) {
                    showTyping();
                    // Retry up to 60s while model loads
                    const waitResult = await waitForModel(60);
                    hideTyping();
                    if (!waitResult) {
                        addBotMsg('? The AI model is still loading. Please wait a moment and try again.');
                        isBusy = false;
                        sendBtn.disabled = false;
                        return;
                    }
                }

                showTyping();

                try {
                    // Build messages array with system prompt + full history
                    const engineMessages = [
                        { role: 'system', content: SYSTEM_PROMPT },
                        ...history.slice(-10),  // last 10 turns for context
                    ];

                    // Stream the response token-by-token
                    const stream = await engine.chat.completions.create({
                        messages: engineMessages,
                        stream: true,
                        max_tokens: 300,
                        temperature: 0.72,
                        top_p: 0.9,
                    });

                    hideTyping();

                    // Create streaming bubble
                    const botBubbleWrap = createBubble('bot', '');
                    messages.appendChild(botBubbleWrap);
                    const botBubble = botBubbleWrap.querySelector('.ps-msg-bubble');
                    let fullReply = '';

                    for await (const chunk of stream) {
                        const token = chunk.choices[0]?.delta?.content || '';
                        fullReply += token;
                        botBubble.innerHTML = renderMarkdown(fullReply);
                        scrollBottom();
                    }

                    // Save assistant response to history
                    history.push({ role: 'assistant', content: fullReply });

                } catch (err) {
                    hideTyping();
                    addBotMsg('?? Something went wrong with the AI. Please try again.');
                    console.error('WebLLM chat error:', err);
                }

                isBusy = false;
                sendBtn.disabled = false;
                input.focus();
            }

            // Poll until model is ready or timeout
            function waitForModel(maxSeconds) {
                return new Promise(resolve => {
                    let elapsed = 0;
                    const timer = setInterval(() => {
                        elapsed++;
                        if (modelReady) { clearInterval(timer); resolve(true); }
                        if (elapsed >= maxSeconds) { clearInterval(timer); resolve(false); }
                    }, 1000);
                });
            }

            // -- Event Listeners ----------------------------------------------
            sendBtn.addEventListener('click', () => sendMessage(input.value));

            input.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    sendMessage(input.value);
                }
            });

            document.querySelectorAll('.ps-suggestion-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', () => sendMessage(btn.dataset.msg));
            });

            // -- Helpers ------------------------------------------------------
            function scrollBottom() {
                setTimeout(() => { messages.scrollTop = messages.scrollHeight; }, 50);
            }

            function setHeaderStatus(html) {
                if (headerStatus) headerStatus.innerHTML = html;
            }

            function escapeHtml(str) {
                return str.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;');
            }

            function renderMarkdown(text) {
                let html = escapeHtml(text);
                html = html.replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
                html = html.replace(/\*(.+?)\*/g, '<em>$1</em>');
                html = html.replace(/^• (.+)$/gm, '<div style="display:flex;gap:6px;margin:2px 0;"><span style="color:#c0396b;flex-shrink:0;">•</span><span>$1</span></div>');
                html = html.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
                return html;
            }

        })();
        </script>

        {% endif %}
        {# Global Hidden form for POST actions (Deactivate, Delete, etc.) #}
        <form id="globalPostActionForm" method="POST" style="display:none;">
            <input type="hidden" name="_token" id="globalPostActionToken" value="">
        </form>

        <script>
        function postAction(url, message, csrfToken = null) {
            if (confirm(message)) {
                const form = document.getElementById('globalPostActionForm');
                const tokenInput = document.getElementById('globalPostActionToken');
                
                form.action = url;
                if (csrfToken) {
                    tokenInput.value = csrfToken;
                } else {
                    // Fallback to meta token if available
                    const metaToken = document.querySelector('meta[name="csrf-token"]');
                    if (metaToken) {
                        tokenInput.value = metaToken.getAttribute('content');
                    }
                }
                form.submit();
            }
        }
        </script>
    </body>
</html>

{% extends 'base.html.twig' %}

{% block title %}Medical Blog & Forum вҖ” PinkShield{% endblock %}

{% block stylesheets %}
<style>
    /* в”Җв”Җ Blog Page вҖ“ Dark Futuristic Theme в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

    /* Hero banner */
    .blog-hero {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(192,57,107,0.25) 0%, rgba(168,85,247,0.15) 100%);
        border: 1px solid rgba(192,57,107,0.25);
        border-radius: 18px;
        padding: 36px 40px;
        color: #fff;
        display: flex;
        align-items: center;
        justify-content: space-between;
        flex-wrap: wrap;
        gap: 16px;
        margin-bottom: 28px;
        box-shadow: 0 8px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.4), inset 0 0 60px rgba(192,57,107,0.06);
        position: relative;
        overflow: hidden;
        backdrop-filter: blur(8px);
    }
    .blog-hero::before {
        content: '';
        position: absolute; top: -60px; right: -60px;
        width: 240px; height: 240px; border-radius: 50%;

<script>
    function setReplyTo(id, name) {
        document.getElementById('parent_comment_id').value = id;
        document.getElementById('reply-to-name').innerText = name;
        document.getElementById('reply-info').classList.remove('d-none');
        document.getElementById('form-title').innerText = 'Reply to ' + name;
        document.querySelector('#comment-form-section').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
        document.getElementById('comment-textarea').focus();
    }

    function cancelReply() {
        document.getElementById('parent_comment_id').value = '';
        document.getElementById('reply-info').classList.add('d-none');
        document.getElementById('form-title').innerText = 'Join the Conversation';
    }
</script>
{% endblock %}

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Activity Chart
    const ctx = document.getElementById('activityChart');
    if (!ctx) return;

    const labels = ['Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat','Sun'];
    const data1 = [12, 19, 14, 22, 18, 28, 24];
    const data2 = [8,  13, 9,  16, 14, 20, 17];

    new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'line',
        data: {
            labels,
            datasets: [{
                label: 'Appointments',
                data: data1,
                borderColor: '#3b82f6',
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(59,130,246,0.08)',
                borderWidth: 2.5,
                pointRadius: 4,
                pointBackgroundColor: '#3b82f6',
                tension: 0.4, fill: true,
            }, {
                label: 'Registrations',
                data: data2,
                borderColor: '#8b5cf6',
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(139,92,246,0.06)',
                borderWidth: 2,
                pointRadius: 3,
                pointBackgroundColor: '#8b5cf6',
                tension: 0.4, fill: true,
            }]
        },
        options: {
            responsive: true,
            maintainAspectRatio: false,
            plugins: {
                legend: { labels: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.5)', font: { size: 11 } } },
                tooltip: {
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(4,12,30,0.95)',
                    borderColor: 'rgba(59,130,246,0.3)',
                    borderWidth: 1,
                    titleColor: '#fff',
                    bodyColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.7)',
                }
            },
            scales: {
                x: {
                    grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)' },
                    ticks: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.35)', font: { size: 11 } }
                },
                y: {
                    grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)' },
                    ticks: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.35)', font: { size: 11 } }
                }
            }
        }
    });
});
</script>

                {{ form_widget(form._token) }}
                    {% if form.vars.errors|length > 0 %}

                            </ul>
                        </div>
                    {% endif %}

                            <div class="invalid-feedback d-block">
                                {% for error in form.email.vars.errors %}
                                    {{ error.message }}
                                {% endfor %}
                            </div>
                        {% endif %}
                    </div>

    /* Error messages handled by AJAX only */
    .invalid-feedback {
        display: none !important;

        color: #dc3545;
        font-size: 0.85rem;

        display: block !important;

    .form-select.is-invalid {
        border-color: #dc3545;
        background-color: #B8E6DB;
    }

{% block javascripts %}
<script>
/* Client-side patient search */
const searchInput = document.getElementById('patientSearch');
if (searchInput) {
    searchInput.addEventListener('input', function () {
        const q = this.value.toLowerCase();
        document.querySelectorAll('#patientsTable tbody tr').forEach(row => {
            const text = row.textContent.toLowerCase();
            row.style.display = text.includes(q) ? '' : 'none';
        });
    });
}
</script>
{% endblock %}

<script>
/* в”Җв”Җ Time Ago в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function timeAgo(date) {
    const seconds = Math.floor((Date.now() - date.getTime()) / 1000);
    const intervals = [
        { label: 'year',   secs: 31536000 },
        { label: 'month',  secs: 2592000 },
        { label: 'week',   secs: 604800 },
        { label: 'day',    secs: 86400 },
        { label: 'hour',   secs: 3600 },
        { label: 'minute', secs: 60 },
    ];
    for (const i of intervals) {
        const count = Math.floor(seconds / i.secs);
        if (count >= 1) return `${count} ${i.label}${count > 1 ? 's' : ''} ago`;
    }
    return 'Just now';
}

document.querySelectorAll('.timeago').forEach(el => {
    const d = new Date(el.getAttribute('datetime'));
    if (!isNaN(d)) el.textContent = timeAgo(d);
});

/* в”Җв”Җ Filter в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function filterNotifs(type, btn) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.filter-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
    btn.classList.add('active');
    document.querySelectorAll('.notif-card').forEach(card => {
        card.style.display = (type === 'all' || card.dataset.type === type) ? '' : 'none';
    });
}

/* в”Җв”Җ Mark Single Read в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function markRead(btn, id) {
    if (btn.classList.contains('done')) return;
    fetch('{{ path("notification_mark_read", {id: 0}) }}'.replace('0', id), {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
    })
    .then(r => r.json())
    .then(data => {
        if (data.success) {
            const card = btn.closest('.notif-card');
            card.classList.remove('unread');
            btn.classList.add('done');
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i>';
            btn.disabled = true;
            updateUnreadStat(-1);
        }
    });
}

/* в”Җв”Җ Mark All Read в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function markAllRead() {
    const btn = document.getElementById('markAllBtn');
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Marking...';

    fetch('{{ path("notification_mark_all_read") }}', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
    })
    .then(r => r.json())
    .then(data => {
        if (data.success) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.notif-card.unread').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('unread'));
            document.querySelectorAll('.btn-read').forEach(b => {
                b.classList.add('done');
                b.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i>';
                b.disabled = true;
            });
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-double"></i> All Done!';
            document.getElementById('unreadStat').textContent = '0';
        }
    })
    .catch(() => {
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-double"></i> Mark All Read';
    });
}

/* в”Җв”Җ Delete в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function deleteNotif(btn, id) {
    if (!confirm('Delete this notification?')) return;
    const card = btn.closest('.notif-card');
    card.classList.add('removing');

    fetch('{{ path("notification_delete", {id: 0}) }}'.replace('0', id), {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
    })
    .then(r => r.json())
    .then(data => {
        if (data.success) {
            setTimeout(() => card.remove(), 300);
            if (card.classList.contains('unread')) updateUnreadStat(-1);
        }
    });
}

/* в”Җв”Җ Helpers в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function updateUnreadStat(delta) {
    const el = document.getElementById('unreadStat');
    if (el) el.textContent = Math.max(0, parseInt(el.textContent || '0') + delta);
}
</script>
{% endblock %}

<script>
/* в”Җв”Җ Time Ago в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
(function() {
    function timeAgo(date) {
        const secs = Math.floor((Date.now() - date.getTime()) / 1000);
        const intervals = [
            { l: 'year',  s: 31536000 }, { l: 'month', s: 2592000 },
            { l: 'week',  s: 604800 },   { l: 'day',   s: 86400 },
            { l: 'hour',  s: 3600 },     { l: 'minute',s: 60 },
        ];
        for (const i of intervals) {
            const c = Math.floor(secs / i.s);
            if (c >= 1) return `${c} ${i.l}${c > 1 ? 's' : ''} ago`;
        }
        return 'Just now';
    }
    document.querySelectorAll('.timeago').forEach(el => {
        const d = new Date(el.getAttribute('datetime'));
        if (!isNaN(d)) el.textContent = timeAgo(d);
    });
})();

{% if not notification.isRead %}
/* в”Җв”Җ Mark Read в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function markThisRead() {
    const btn = document.getElementById('markBtn');
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Marking...';

    fetch('{{ path("notification_mark_read", {id: notification.id}) }}', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
    })
    .then(r => r.json())
    .then(data => {
        if (data.success) {
            btn.className = 'btn btn-mark done';
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> Read';
            const badge = document.getElementById('readBadge');
            badge.className = 'badge-pill is-read';
            badge.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> Read';
        }
    });
}
{% endif %}

/* в”Җв”Җ Delete в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function deleteThis() {
    if (!confirm('Delete this notification permanently?')) return;

    fetch('{{ path("notification_delete", {id: notification.id}) }}', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
    })
    .then(r => r.json())
    .then(data => {
        if (data.success) window.location.href = '{{ path("notifications_index") }}';
    });
}
</script>

<script>
    // Search functionality
    document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('keyup', function() {
        const searchTerm = this.value.toLowerCase();
        const products = document.querySelectorAll('.product-card');
        
        products.forEach(product => {
            const productName = product.getAttribute('data-product-name');
            if (productName.includes(searchTerm)) {
                product.style.display = '';
            } else {
                product.style.display = 'none';
            }
        });
    });

    // Modal functions
    function showProductDetails(id, name, price, description) {
        document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = name;
        document.getElementById('modalDescription').textContent = description;
        document.getElementById('modalPrice').textContent = '$' + price;
        document.getElementById('productModal').style.display = 'block';
    }

    function closeProductDetails() {
        document.getElementById('productModal').style.display = 'none';
    }

    // Close modal when clicking outside
    document.getElementById('productModal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (e.target === this) {
            this.style.display = 'none';
        }
    });

    // Wishlist functionality
    function toggleWishlist(button, productId) {
        // Prevent multiple clicks during request
        if (button.disabled) return;
        
        button.disabled = true;
        const isInWishlist = button.classList.contains('in-wishlist');
        const url = isInWishlist 
            ? `{{ path('wishlist_remove_by_product', {productId: 0}) }}`.replace('0', productId)
            : `{{ path('wishlist_add', {productId: 0}) }}`.replace('0', productId);
        
        // Get CSRF token from meta tag
        const csrfToken = document.querySelector('meta[name="csrf-token"]')?.getAttribute('content') || '';
        
        fetch(url, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest',
                'X-CSRF-TOKEN': csrfToken
            }
        })
        .then(response => response.json())
        .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
                if (isInWishlist) {
                    button.classList.remove('in-wishlist');
                } else {
                    button.classList.add('in-wishlist');
                }
            } else {
                console.error('Error:', data.message);
            }
        })
        .catch(error => {
            console.error('Error:', error);
            // Revert on error
            if (isInWishlist) {
                button.classList.add('in-wishlist');
            } else {
                button.classList.remove('in-wishlist');
            }
        })
        .finally(() => {
            button.disabled = false;
        });
    }

    // Initialize wishlist buttons on page load
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const wishlistButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.wishlist-btn');
        wishlistButtons.forEach(button => {
            const productId = button.dataset.productId;
            fetch(`{{ path('wishlist_check', {productId: 0}) }}`.replace('0', productId))
                .then(response => response.json())
                .then(data => {
                    if (data.inWishlist) {
                        button.classList.add('in-wishlist');
                    }
                })
                .catch(error => console.error('Error:', error));
        });
    });
</script>
{% endblock %}

{% block javascripts %}
<script>
function updateSlider(name, value) {
    const badge = document.getElementById(name + '-val');
    if (badge) badge.textContent = value;

    const input = document.getElementById(name);
    if (input) {
        const min = parseFloat(input.min) || 0;
        const max = parseFloat(input.max) || 10;
        const pct = ((parseFloat(value) - min) / (max - min)) * 100;
        input.style.background =
            `linear-gradient(to right, var(--primary) 0%, var(--primary) ${pct}%, #e5e7eb ${pct}%, #e5e7eb 100%)`;
    }
}

/* Init all sliders on load */
document.querySelectorAll('input[type="range"]').forEach(input => {
    updateSlider(input.name, input.value);
});
</script>
{% endblock %}

            <i class="fas fa-exclamation-circle"></i>
