            <i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i>
        {% endif %}
    </div>
    <div class="suggestion-body">
        <h3>
            {% if sLevel == 'urgent' %}вҡ пёҸ Attention Recommended
            {% elseif sLevel == 'warning' %}рҹ’ӣ Health Notice
            {% else %}вң… You're Doing Well
            {% endif %}
            {% if sLevel != 'ok' %}
                <span class="score-badge {{ sLevel }}"><i class="fas fa-chart-bar"></i> Risk score: {{ suggestion.score }}/14</span>
            {% endif %}
        </h3>
        <p>{{ suggestion.message }}</p>

        {# Reason chips #}

            {% for reason in suggestion.reasons %}

            {% endfor %}
        </div>
        {% endif %}

            </span>

{% block javascripts %}
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js@4.4.0/dist/chart.umd.min.js"></script>
<script>
/* в”Җв”Җ Slider update helper в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function updateSlider(name, value) {
    const badge = document.getElementById(name + '-val');
    if (badge) badge.textContent = value;

    const input = document.getElementById(name);
    if (input) {
        const min = parseFloat(input.min) || 0;
        const max = parseFloat(input.max) || 10;
        const pct = ((parseFloat(value) - min) / (max - min)) * 100;
        input.style.background =
            `linear-gradient(to right, var(--primary) 0%, var(--primary) ${pct}%, #e5e7eb ${pct}%, #e5e7eb 100%)`;
    }

    // Trigger live risk analysis on every slider change
    analyzeRisk();
}

/* в”Җв”Җ Real-time Risk Analysis в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
function analyzeRisk() {
    const val = id => parseFloat(document.getElementById(id)?.value || 0);

    const stress    = val('stress');
    const mood      = val('mood');
    const anxiety   = val('anxiety_level');
    const sleep     = val('sleep_hours');
    const energy    = val('energy_level');
    const motivation = val('motivation_level');

    let score = 0;
    let reasons = [];

    if (stress >= 8)       { score += 3; reasons.push('Very high stress'); }
    else if (stress >= 6)  { score += 1; reasons.push('Elevated stress'); }

    if (mood <= 3)         { score += 3; reasons.push('Very low mood'); }
    else if (mood <= 5)    { score += 1; reasons.push('Low mood'); }

    if (anxiety >= 7)      { score += 2; reasons.push('High anxiety'); }
    else if (anxiety >= 5) { score += 1; reasons.push('Moderate anxiety'); }

    if (sleep > 0 && sleep < 4)         { score += 2; reasons.push('Very low sleep'); }
    else if (sleep >= 4 && sleep < 6)   { score += 1; reasons.push('Low sleep'); }

    if (energy > 0 && energy <= 2)      { score += 2; reasons.push('Critically low energy'); }
    else if (energy > 2 && energy <= 4) { score += 1; reasons.push('Low energy'); }

    if (motivation > 0 && motivation <= 2) { score += 1; reasons.push('Very low motivation'); }

    const alert   = document.getElementById('liveAlert');
    const alertMsg = document.getElementById('liveAlertMsg');
    const alertBtn = document.getElementById('liveAlertBtn');

    if (!alert) return;

    // Remove existing level classes
    alert.classList.remove('show', 'lvl-warning', 'lvl-urgent');
    alertBtn.style.display = 'none';

    if (score >= 5) {
        alert.classList.add('show', 'lvl-urgent');
        alertMsg.textContent = `вҡ пёҸ Current inputs suggest high health risk (score: ${score}/14) вҖ” ${reasons.slice(0,2).join(', ')}. Consider booking an appointment.`;
        alertBtn.textContent = 'рҹ“… Book Now';
        alertBtn.style.cssText = 'display:inline-flex;margin-left:auto;white-space:nowrap;font-size:0.8rem;padding:5px 12px;border-radius:7px;text-decoration:none;font-weight:700;background:#ef4444;color:#fff;';
    } else if (score >= 2) {
        alert.classList.add('show', 'lvl-warning');
        alertMsg.textContent = `рҹ’ӣ Some concern detected (score: ${score}/14) вҖ” ${reasons.join(', ')}.`;
        alertBtn.textContent = 'рҹ“… Book Consultation';
        alertBtn.style.cssText = 'display:inline-flex;margin-left:auto;white-space:nowrap;font-size:0.8rem;padding:5px 12px;border-radius:7px;text-decoration:none;font-weight:700;background:#f59e0b;color:#fff;';
    }
}

/* Init all sliders on page load */
document.querySelectorAll('input[type="range"]').forEach(input => {
    updateSlider(input.name, input.value);
});

/* в”Җв”Җ Weekly Chart в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
{% if weeklyData|length > 0 %}
const weeklyLabels = [
    {% for item in weeklyData %}
        "{{ item.date|date('d/m') }}",
    {% endfor %}
];
const moodData = [{% for item in weeklyData %}{{ item.mood ? item.mood|number_format(1) : 'null' }},{% endfor %}];
const stressData = [{% for item in weeklyData %}{{ item.stress ? item.stress|number_format(1) : 'null' }},{% endfor %}];
const energyData = [{% for item in weeklyData %}{{ item.energy ? item.energy|number_format(1) : 'null' }},{% endfor %}];

const ctx = document.getElementById('weeklyChart').getContext('2d');
new Chart(ctx, {
    type: 'line',
    data: {
        labels: weeklyLabels,
        datasets: [
            {
                label: 'Mood',
                data: moodData,
                borderColor: '#f59e0b',
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(245,158,11,0.08)',
                borderWidth: 2.5,
                pointBackgroundColor: '#f59e0b',
                pointRadius: 4,
                pointHoverRadius: 6,
                tension: 0.35,
                fill: true,
            },
            {
                label: 'Stress',
                data: stressData,
                borderColor: '#ef4444',
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(239,68,68,0.08)',
                borderWidth: 2.5,
                pointBackgroundColor: '#ef4444',
                pointRadius: 4,
                pointHoverRadius: 6,
                tension: 0.35,
                fill: true,
            },
            {
                label: 'Energy',

                borderColor: '#3b82f6',
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(59,130,246,0.08)',
                borderWidth: 2.5,
                pointBackgroundColor: '#3b82f6',
                pointRadius: 4,
                pointHoverRadius: 6,
                tension: 0.35,
                fill: true,
            }
        ]
    },
    options: {
        responsive: true,
        maintainAspectRatio: false,
        interaction: { mode: 'index', intersect: false },
        plugins: {
            legend: {
                position: 'top',
                labels: {
                    font: { size: 11, weight: '600', family: 'Inter' },
                    usePointStyle: true,
                    pointStyleWidth: 8,
                    padding: 16,
                }
            },
            tooltip: {
                backgroundColor: '#fff',

                }
            }
        },
        scales: {
            x: {
                grid: { display: false },

<script>
    function removeFromWishlist(button, wishlistId) {
        if (confirm('Are you sure you want to remove this item from your wishlist?')) {
            fetch(`{{ path('wishlist_remove', {wishlistId: 0}) }}`.replace('0', wishlistId), {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                }
            })
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (data.success) {
                    const row = button.closest('tr');
                    row.style.opacity = '0.5';
                    row.style.textDecoration = 'line-through';
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        row.remove();
                        // Refresh total via API
                        refreshTotal();
                        // Refresh page if empty
                        if (document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr').length === 0) {
                            location.reload();
                        }
                    }, 300);
                }
            });
        }
    }

    function refreshTotal() {
        fetch('{{ path('wishlist_api_total') }}')
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (data.success) {
                    const totalEl = document.getElementById('wishlist-total');
                    if (totalEl) {
                        totalEl.textContent = parseFloat(data.totalPrice).toFixed(2);
                    }
                }
            })
            .catch(err => console.error('Failed to refresh total:', err));
    }

    function buyProduct(productId, productName) {
        alert('Thank you for your interest in ' + productName + '! Purchase feature coming soon.');
    }
</script>

{% endblock %}
